name:S‚Äçt‚Äçe‚Äçv‚Äçe‚Äçn
info:Guestroom (2 beds)
info:Stayed in July 2022
info:Friends
info:5 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted July 22, 2022
msg:Although we only stayed for one evening it was a most pleasurable one.  I have very basic Chinese language skills (i.e. None) but the staff were very patient and helpful. It also helped that I had taken a Chinese friend with me for the short break. 
Check in was swift and only took around 5 minutes considering I needed to provide all my documentation and covid codes etc. Again the staff were great an made us feel very welcome.

The room was huge with two almost Double beds, a huge bathroom and giant circular bathtub as well as a shower. The mini bar was well stocked and there was a dressing room as well as robes, slippers etc. After a few minutes settling in we were treated to a gift of fresh fruit which was very much appreciated.

The beds were super comfortable and we slept well after we returned from an evening out in Tonglu.

In the morning the breakfast was typical Chinese buffet and was delicious though we didn't eat too much due to our previous evenings dinner.  

Even though I was clearly the only Westerner in the Hotel at that point I was made to feel very welcome by every single person I encountered....both staff and guests.

I would highly recommend a stay here if you should ever visit Tonglu.
